The City Public Security Bureau Detective Team Cracks Down on a Large-Scale Drug Pellet Organization - Confiscating More Than Ten Large Burlap Bags of White Powder Raw Materials - Four Large Boxes of Finished Red Pills and Other Supplies - The Main Culprits Liu Zheng Han Li Hou Shan and Others Have Been Arrested

Lu Ying, the director of the Detective Division of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, suddenly received a secret report at 7:00 am yesterday, stating that someone had set up a large-scale distribution center for drug pellets in the house at No. 5 Gaoxiangtou, which is under the jurisdiction of the Third Branch of the First District. Please send personnel to arrest them as soon as possible. After receiving the report, Lu immediately sent Leader Chen Caifu, along with a large number of detectives, to seize the place. As a result, a large box of red pills was seized on the spot, and Liu Zheng Han and Yu Zhanhe were arrested and brought to the team for interrogation. After the two criminals confessed that the manufacturing center was located at No. 72 Sanminfang, near Haichao Temple, Dongpuyu Road, the original detectives went straight to the Sanminfang house. The center was heavily guarded, but as a result, all the detectives seized the place one by one, totaling more than ten large burlap bags of white powder raw materials for making pills, four large boxes of finished red pills, three large writing desk-style heating ovens, several iron boxes of sugar powder, three large wooden trays, and a large number of other items used for making pills. The criminals Li Hou Shan, Huang Hanqing, Wang Jinsheng, and the woman Wang Li Shi were arrested on the spot. The items and criminals were transported to the team one by one by car. After Director Lu interrogated them one by one, they all admitted to manufacturing and selling them in this city and other places without hesitation. Director Wen was extremely furious upon hearing the news, believing that the criminals dared to set up a center so close to the bureau, which was extremely illegal. He has ordered a strict investigation.

Another Assassin of Tang Jiapeng Has Been Identified - Zhao Guangfu, a Native of Yangzhou - Admits to the Assassination of Tang Without Hesitation

Tang Jiapeng, the manager of the Rongji Game Hall in the Great World, was suddenly assassinated and killed by thugs in front of the Great World at around 2:00 am on June 18th of this year. An unnamed man was also killed by stray bullets. After the case occurred, the police authorities of the French Concession paid close attention to the investigation and arrest of the criminals. On the morning of the 28th of last month, Jin Jiulin, the superintendent of the special agency of the French Police, led the detectives on duty, along with Chinese and Western detectives from the Gordon Road Police Station, to arrest a criminal, Zhang Tinggui, also known as Zhang Xiaosizi, a native of Funing, at a stove shop at No. 648 Haifang Road, West Shanghai. He was escorted to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. All the details have been reported in the previous news. The superintendent Jin Jiulin and others also found out that Zhang Tinggui's accomplice, Zhao Guangfu, a native of Yangzhou, was arrested by the Chinese and Western detectives of the Putuo Road Police Station on the 22nd of the same month for carrying a pistol and bullets while passing through Putuo Road in the Public Concession. It was found that he had also committed a robbery case and was escorted to the First Special District Court for trial. On July 24th, Zhao was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment and is currently serving his sentence in the First Special District Prison. The Western Police Chief was immediately reported and transferred to the Second Special District Court to prepare a document. The superintendent Jin led detectives Qian Yumin, Liu Dianlong, Wang Wannian, etc., to the First Special District Court the day before yesterday to transfer Zhao Guangfu to the French Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court. Judge Zhang Chaozuo was promoted to preside over the trial. First, the police lawyer Yao Zhao presented the case, stating briefly that the defendant Zhao Guangfu was an accomplice in the assassination of Tang Jiapeng. He was arrested by the Public Concession Police for possessing military firearms and was sentenced to imprisonment by the Special First Court. The police department has investigated and transferred him to the case. The police station has not yet thoroughly investigated the case due to time constraints, and the previously arrested criminal Zhang Tinggui has been rescheduled by the court to be tried on the 13th of this month. It is requested that the defendant be detained temporarily and rescheduled to be tried together with the Zhang Tinggui case after the case is investigated. Upon interrogation, the defendant Zhao Guangfu confessed that he was 28 years old, from Yangzhou, and worked as a carpenter. He used to live in a thatched shed on Pushan Road, Zhabei. He admitted to jointly assassinating Tang Jiapeng. He was invited by Carpenter Zhou Ermu to help. Two days earlier, they agreed to discuss the matter at a stove shop on Hengfeng Road, Zhabei. I went at 11:00 am, but they had already left. Later, they agreed to go to the stove shop again at 8:00 pm the next night and promised to give me 100 yuan after the matter was completed. On the night of the incident, Zhou hired a rickshaw in Zhabei to transport the pistol to the red tin-wrapped cigarette clock opposite the Great World to wait. I went at 1:00 am. Zhou gave me a pistol, and Zhang Tinggui and others waited at the entrance of the Great World together. When Tang came out, I fired three shots at the back of the car and fled. But I did not receive a penny afterwards. After verifying the confession in court, the defendant was ordered to be returned to custody and rescheduled to be tried together with Zhang Tinggui on the 13th.

News of the Second Major Chess Game Between China, the United States, Britain, and Russia - The Previous Game Had Not Been Decided

Chess masters from China, the United States, Britain, and Russia held their second international chess game at the YMCA on Eight Immortals Bridge last night. The notary was Mr. Danai Pan from Portugal. The British, American, and Russian federations included Di Tuigen from Britain, Cui Yi from Russia, and Toping from the United States (represented by Mr. Shiba). China was represented by Pan Jishi, Xie Xiazun, and You Pengxi. The two sides sat at a table together and played against each other. During the opening ceremony, Wang Jianxian, the executive of the YMCA, reported everything, and then the competition began, and the competition was fierce. As a result, the federation won. The previous game (won by China) had not been decided. It is known that the next game plans to separate each team member one by one and use a metronome to urge the game (that is, each person must make a move every minute to determine the final victory).

Wu Tiecheng's Speech at the Lianhuan Club - Shanghai Has Two Major Dangers

The Shanghai Lianhuan Club held a public banquet last night in honor of its member Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of Shanghai, who also served as the Songhu Garrison Commander. Members Wang Yansong, Yang Hu, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Liu Hongsheng, Xu Peihuang, Wen Hongen, Jiang Qun, Zhang Danru, Wang Boyuan, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Wu Kaixian, Dai Gengxin, Yuan Ludeng, Tao Baichuan, Ding Mocun, Wen Jiangang, Zhu Wenqi, Lu Zhongxian, Sun Xueni, Qian Longzhang, Chen Ziming, Jiang Zhigang, Yu Guozhen, Hu Guocheng, Xie Pengfei, Jiang Yichun, Pan Xusheng, Tao Changhai, Zheng Zenan, Ye Jiaxing, Hu Xiyuan, Geng Jizhi, Jin Runxiang, Zhou Bangjun, Lu Wenshao, Lu Jingshi, Dong Yu, Wu Kaisheng, Zhu Shaoping, Wu Zhihao, and Sun Mingqi attended the banquet, totaling more than 60 people. During the banquet, Chairman Wang Xiaolai and Wang Tingsong stood up to give speeches, followed by a speech by Mayor Wu. He briefly stated that he was very grateful for the invitation to the public banquet. He was ordered to lead Shanghai at a time of crisis and shock in the city. Fortunately, with the understanding and mutual assistance of old friends from the club and local people, he was able to pass through smoothly. He felt that he was not competent enough to serve as the Songhu Garrison Commander at the same time. He hoped that his fellow club members would give him advice from time to time. However, he deeply felt that Shanghai was a trading place and a major port. The prosperity and decline of Shanghai should be based on the prosperity and decline of the interior. Now, the rural areas in the interior are bankrupt and the economy is exhausted. The increase in Shanghai's population is faster than any city in the world, and the accumulation of cash in Shanghai is also more than any city in the world. This kind of畸形 development actually hides infinite crises, just like a fish will inevitably dry up when the source of water dries up. Therefore, people in Shanghai should find ways to revive the rural areas and enrich the interior to cultivate their source. All of you here are leaders from all walks of life. I hope you will shoulder this important task and work with people from all walks of life to work hard to revive the rural movement to reduce the crisis in Shanghai. This is one of the dangers. Currently, people from all over the world say that the Second World War will break out in 1936, and some say it will begin in 1937 or 1938. This is not only what Chinese people think, but also what Europeans and Americans speculate. We certainly do not want to confirm when the war will happen, but if a war does happen, its location will be in two places: either in the Pacific Ocean or in the Siberian region. If it happens in the Pacific Ocean, Shanghai will be the center and will inevitably be ravaged. If it happens in the Siberian region, Shanghai will also be implicated. However, how to resist the coming disaster? The 400 million compatriots should gather their strength and prepare urgently for self-rescue under the leadership of the Chinese Kuomintang. The way to self-rescue is nothing more than stabilizing the interior first. Now the government is urgently recovering the bandit areas, which is also to stabilize the interior and enrich the national power. People in Shanghai cannot stand idly by and should assist the government in suppressing the red bandits as an act of self-rescue and saving the country. This is the second danger. The Chinese Kuomintang and the Chinese Kuomintang government have had things that have not satisfied the people due to the actions of a few bad elements in the past, but the Chinese Kuomintang has suffered from unprecedented national disasters in history and still bears its responsibility. It can be worthy of heaven and earth. I hope that all club members will work together to overcome this difficult situation. Then he raised a glass to wish all the club members well. Wu Kaixian, a standing committee member of the Municipal Party Department, then gave a speech on the tragic situation in the bandit areas of Jiangxi. The words were too long to be recorded.

The Police Trainee School Will Commence Classes; New Police Examination Papers Completely Marked

The Municipal Police Bureau is holding a police trainee school, and the preparatory committee previously established within the old county office on Penglai Road recruited student police officers. A written examination was also held at Wan Zhu Elementary School in Nine Acres the other day. After a short selection process, the training will begin soon. The school is located in Gaochang Temple, which has ample space. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables the Executive Yuan, Requesting Correction of Vegetable Cattle Taxation; Taxing by Head is Equivalent to the Revival of Likin

Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance, requesting correction of the Jiangsu Province's proposal to tax vegetable cattle. The original telegram stated: "To the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance: Having received a letter from the Cattle and Sheep Trade Association stating that the 'Provisional Regulations of Jiangsu Province Prohibiting the Trafficking and Slaughter of Ploughing Cattle' have been promulgated recently and will be implemented soon. However, Article 3 of the regulations stipulates that vegetable cattle slaughtered or trafficked should be taxed at a fixed rate, with detailed rules to be determined separately by the Departments of Civil Affairs, Finance, and Construction. A copy of the regulations is enclosed for your review. Jiangsu was originally a province where likin was abolished. Recently, Minister Kong took office and declared that no new taxes would be added to reassure our people. Now, Jiangsu Province suddenly levies this new tax, which conflicts with the tax regulations. Please telegraph to argue against it.' After likin was abolished, the only goods taxed were the import, export, and transit duties of the customs, as well as the consolidated tax, tobacco and alcohol tax, and salt tax, all of which fall under the jurisdiction of the central government. The only tax under the jurisdiction of the provincial government is the business tax, which is a behavior tax and not a tax on goods. That is why it differs from likin. Now, Jiangsu Province plans to tax the sale of vegetable cattle by head, which violates the central government's tax system and is equivalent to the revival of likin. We hereby respectfully request your esteemed Yuan (Ministry) to review and correct this matter to maintain the overall abolition of likin and avoid extra-legal burdens, as it is for the public convenience." The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce kowtows.

Huizhou People Telegraph Requesting Exemption from Increased Salt Tax

The Huining Native Association in Shanghai has received reports from various counties in Xiuning, Yi, Qi, and Wu in recent days, stating that salt in Huizhou has been subject to an additional tax of one yuan per dan, as ordered by the Liangzhe Salt Transport Commissioner. Because Huizhou has suffered from consecutive years of disasters, famine, and banditry, the people's hardships have reached an extreme. Salt is a necessity of life, and the sudden increase in such a heavy tax will cause difficulties for merchants and the people in food supply. The life of the people will be unimaginable. Moreover, this tax increase is only applied to Xiuning and Yi (Xiuning's salt is drawn from the Xiu area, and Qi's salt is drawn from the Yi area), while Shexian is exempt, which is unfair. The association requests an appeal to exempt the increase, so as to reduce the burden. After receiving the report, the association telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, the Salt Affairs Department, and the Liangzhe Salt Transport Commissioner yesterday, requesting them to consider the people's difficulties and grant exemption. It also sent letters to the public groups in each county to jointly strive for a resolution to maximize its effect.

Xu's "Kitchen Talk" Pearl Returns to the World

The book "Kitchen Talk," written by Xu Guangqi, the Ming Dynasty Grand Secretary from Shanghai, was a defense strategy to protect the Han people. It was banned and destroyed during the Qing Dynasty, but a copy was preserved in the National Library of Paris. This year, November 24th, marks the 300th anniversary of Xu Guangqi's death. The Xujiahui Catholic Magazine entrusted a friend to make a photographic print and send it back, and the pearl has returned from overseas. The Tushanwan Printing House is reprinting it using high-quality Lian Shi paper and large font. The book consists of five volumes, bound in two books, and costs $1.50, with an additional 10% for postage. It can be purchased from the magazine. The magazine also sells the reprinted "Xu Wending Gong Bi Ji," which has been well preserved after three centuries of war. It sells for $0.60.

Electric Company Employee Chen Qinglu's Condition Recovers

Chen Qinglu, an employee of the Shanghai Electric Power Company, was suddenly shot and injured by thugs on the morning of the 20th of last month. After careful treatment by Dr. Hou Yunqing of Sacred Heart Hospital and assistance from Dr. Niu Huilin, the wounds on his head, chest, and back have gradually healed. The bullet remaining in his thigh was also removed by Dr. Hou using surgery yesterday morning (the 8th), and his recovery is progressing well.

The Soon-to-Open Greater Shanghai Theater Boasts Magnificent and Unparalleled Architecture and the Most Valuable Films

The much-anticipated Greater Shanghai Theater has been under construction for a year and a half, with day and night work to rush completion. It has recently been completed, and its decorations and equipment are luxurious and novel, making it a standout in Shanghai. The style adopted throughout the building, from the facade to the screen, the roof to the floor, is a complete design, with no contradictory elements. The front wall is

Black Glass

Clean, quiet, and unprecedented, interspersed with eight light green glass pillars, majestic and well-proportioned, further enhancing its appearance. At night, the radiance is emitted in all directions, elegant and pleasing. Located near Nicheng Bridge, the city opens its doors to a nightlife. The entrance hall is spacious, and the floors and escalators are all

Paved with Rubber

With elasticity, walking on it is silent, and the patterns and colors echo the interior design. It is said that this type of rubber flooring is a recent invention, and the Greater Shanghai Theater is the first to use it. In the future, even if the audience is extremely crowded, there will be no risk of slipping. The theater has

Over 1,700 Seats

All with spring cushions and floral silk seat covers. The size and style have been studied for two months and modified seven or eight times before they were finalized. The features, such as the deepened cushions and the numbers on the front, are all original and unconventional. The four walls use the latest invention of non-combustible

Sound-Absorbing Paper Board

With fine holes on it, it can absorb sound waves. Therefore, the dialogues and songs emitted from the screen can be clearly heard in the farthest and most remote seats in the theater, with no echo problems at all. The theater's sound system is the Ersi Ai

Huge Sound Machine

It includes the latest improved features, arrived this month, and is being installed. The sound is clear, with no noise. Combined with the theater's equipment, it is even more perfect and beautiful. The aisles in the theater are all covered with

Thick Wool Carpets

Which benefits the sound and enhances the grandeur. The colors and patterns were also designed by experts and specially made by Tianjin carpet merchants to the highest standards. Other advantages are too numerous to mention due to space limitations. It is said that the theater has signed

Exclusive Screening Contracts

With the American Fox and RKO companies, the first-run screening rights of all films produced by these two companies will be held by the theater. Fox and RKO are both giants in the American film industry. The theater has both, so it is conceivable that there will be many blockbusters after the opening. Currently, the theater is actively arranging the interior and will open as soon as it is ready. In about a month, the men and women of Shanghai will be able to feast their eyes.

Hong Kong Happy Valley Fresh Olives 丨Xing Hua Lou Distributes 丨

The sandalwood olive is produced in Fujian, Guangdong, and other places. Its taste is sweet and palatable, and it is beneficial to the throat and can eliminate coal toxins. Everyone knows and loves to eat it. Recently, it has become popular in the market. However, ordinary olives are bitter and astringent, so those who are not used to eating them do not like them. It is said that the Hong Kong Tai Po Happy Valley has spared no expense on olives, studying them in detail. It has purchased more than 1,000 mu of land in Tai Po to cultivate more than 100,000 olive trees. After years of research, it has succeeded in completely eliminating the bitterness and astringency, obtaining a clear, fragrant, and crispy olive that even those who are not used to eating it can enjoy. It is said that the garden can produce four or five thousand dan of olives each year, which are sold in Hong Kong, Guangdong, Guizhou, and other southern provinces, and are highly praised. Few people in this city know about it. Xing Hua Lou Restaurant on Sima Road has specially reached an agreement with Happy Valley to be the distributor in this city. The olives have now arrived in Shanghai, but the supply is limited. Those who wish to try them should purchase them quickly. The price is set at 45 cents per pound, and wholesale prices are available.

Kidnapping and Theft Cases Interrogated Simultaneously 丨 Sentences to be Pronounced Separately on a Scheduled Date 丨

Zhang Zilin, a Fuyang native and foreman for the Public Works Department, had his four-year-old son, Fu Hai (born to a concubine), kidnapped from his home at 722 Weihaiwei Road at around 6:00 AM on April 27th of last year. The kidnappers entered through the back door, went upstairs, and carried Fu Hai away from his bed. The father heard the alarm and gave chase, but the kidnappers opened fire, wounding Zhang and a maid, Li Tao, who died. The ransom note was hidden in a remote part of Chongming, demanding a large sum. Zhang, over fifty, had only this one son. After paying 40,000 yuan in ransom, the Hongkou Police arrested three suspects and sent them to court, where they were sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment. The ringleader, Xi Shirong, escaped and could not be found. At 7:00 PM on the 13th of last month, Chinese Detectives Wang Chengying and Yang Xiguang of the Jiaxing Road Police arrested more than ten major thieves, including Wang Jinshan and Chen Desheng, at the Xinxing Vegetable Restaurant at 238 Datong Road and at the Nanshi Railway Station. Chen confessed that he and Yan Shirong and others had committed a kidnapping case, which was the kidnapping of Wang Hai, Fu Hai, at 722 Weihaiwei Road. The detectives learned that Yan was Wang's brother-in-law and arrested Yan's wife, Chen, at 11 Tianbao Road, Junan Lane, Zhabei, along with the instigator and accomplices Wang's wife, Yan's son-in-law Xu Yunsun, accountant Xiang Wenshan, and workers Yang Yuexiang and Mu Xiao Sizi. The suspects were sent to the First Special District Court. Chen Desheng and Xiang Wenshan confessed without hesitation, providing detailed accounts of the kidnapping. The others denied any involvement. During the second court hearing, Yan Chen and Xiang Wenshan completely overturned their previous confessions to the police and in court, claiming that they were nonsense. The interrogating officer, considering that Wang Yan, Xu Yunsun, Yang Yuexiang, and Mu Xiao Sizi were proven by the plaintiff Wang Zilin to have little involvement, allowed them to be released on bail. The others were returned to custody. As reported in this newspaper, the Central Police determined that the 13 thieves, including Wang Jinshan, who were arrested by the Putuo Road Police, had used weapons to rob 11 households, including Yu Hengchang at 44 Parker Road and Guo at 755 McGinn Road, between March of last year and October of this year, with property worth over 1,500 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, the police sent the defendants to the Third Criminal Court in two groups. Judge Wu Zehan first interrogated Wang Jinshan and others for the theft case. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin presented the case, and the victims testified about their experiences. The defendants' testimonies were inconsistent, and they were all ordered to be returned to custody. The sentence will be pronounced on the morning of the 11th. The kidnapping case was then heard, and Chen Desheng suddenly denied his involvement, claiming that he was in his hometown of Jiangbei on that day and that his previous confessions to the police and in court were false. Witnesses Xu Asan and Xu Yongming testified that Xiang Wenshan was indeed in Xietang Township, Suzhou, on April 27th, handling fertilizers. Xiang Wenshan and Yan Chen repeated their previous denials. Yang Yuexiang, Mu Xiao Sizi, Wang Yan, and Xu Yunsun insisted that they were falsely accused and requested an investigation. They retained lawyers Fu Ganghou and Huang Xiubo to defend them. Wang Zilin stated that the two kidnappers he saw were around 20 years old, and the shooter was around 30 years old, both being thin. Wang Chen and the others were not seen by him. Wang's child, Jie Hai, is currently ill and away from Shanghai, so even if he were to appear in court, he would not be able to identify them, as he was not yet three years old when he was kidnapped and does not know anything. After the lawyers debated in court, Judge Fang ordered Chen Desheng, Yan Chen, and Xiang Wenshan to be returned to custody, and Yang Yuexiang, Mu Xiao Sizi, Wang Yan, and Xu Yunsun were each released on their original bail. The sentence will be pronounced on the 14th.

The Strongman Cha Ruilong's Family Property Dispute Case 丨 The Grandfather Sold Pancakes and Had No Property 丨 The Current Property Was Created by His Father 丨 The Cousin Sues for Encroachment on Ancestral Property 丨

Cha Ruilong, the strongman actor from the Yihua Film Company, is being sued by his cousin Rui Lian through lawyers Zhu Sifu, Yang Ruinian, and Li Mian at the First Special District Court for occupying over 100,000 yuan of ancestral property and refusing to distribute his cousin's share of 50,000 yuan. The case has been heard once, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Xiangzu opened the Fifth Criminal Court for a hearing. Cha Ruilong and his lawyer Yuan Yang'an were also present. Lawyer Li stated that the plaintiff's previous request for the court to obtain the case files of the property division dispute between the defendant and his sister Xin Yuan from the District Court had not been fulfilled. Judge Wu stated that the case files had not yet been obtained. Cha Rui Lian stated that the ancestral property was worth about 100,000 yuan. His father and uncle never divided it, so he should be entitled to half of it. He is suing because the defendant refuses to hand it over. As evidence, Xin Yuan removed his property from the list after the dispute with the defendant before the division was made. Cha Ruilong testified that his grandfather sold pancakes and left no property. The current property was created by his father. The judge asked if he had said anything about removing the name of Decun (the plaintiff's father) during the dispute with Cha Xinyuan. Cha Ruilong replied that he had not. The judge asked how much Xin Yuan received. He answered that she received one-sixth, about 8,000 yuan. The court stated that the case files from the District Court had not yet been obtained, making it difficult to proceed, and adjourned the hearing for another date.

Wang Pingnan Establishes Jian'er Industrial Cooperative, Locating Anti-Japanese Hero Liang Tongfang, Breaking Free from Rickshaw Pulling and Focusing on Craftsmanship

Liang Tongfang, a Northeastern anti-Japanese hero, had been unemployed since coming to Shanghai. In order to solve his living difficulties, he had been pulling a rickshaw to support himself. Wang Pingnan, the former commander-in-chief of the anti-Japanese volunteer army, heard about this and invited Liang to his residence to inquire about everything. He promised to find him a suitable position to support his life. He learned that Ling Yun, an employee of the Shanghai Guohuo Company, was skilled in making various wax fruits, which sold well in the market, making it a simple and easy small-scale industry. Wang invested several hundred yuan to establish the Jian'er Industrial Cooperative with Ling Yun and invited Liang to work there. In addition, four other anti-Japanese heroes have been prepared and will open soon.

Japanese Thug Arrested for Extortion

The Dahonglou Restaurant at 406 Broadway closed down due to business failure and was being liquidated. The restaurant had equipment and miscellaneous items worth 400 yuan. The court ordered an auction to pay off creditors. The buyers of the above items were Fan Yimin, a Chongming native and used goods merchant; Xie Yongjin, a Ningbo native; and Tao Lianggen and Cai, both from Tongzhou. They went to the restaurant at around 10:00 AM with judicial police to take delivery of the items, issued invoices, and moved various equipment out. Cai and the bailiff went to the court to pay the money. However, Li Asan, a Zhenjiang native; Wang Amao, a Shanghai native; and Zhang Shifu, all local thugs, learned of this and gathered a dozen accomplices to go to the restaurant. Li Asan asked who bought the items. Wang Amao said that they were brothers from the Huishan Road area and there were many of them. They needed 50 yuan for expenses; otherwise, they would not be allowed to take the items away. Xie Yongjin replied that the boss, surnamed Cai, had not returned from paying the money at the court and would inform them when he returned. Zhang Shifu then smashed a handful of parts, a teapot, and two mud statues. Li Asan then punched Xie Yongjin in the chest, knocking him to the ground, and said that he had to pay 50 yuan. Seeing the menacing situation, Fan Yimin blew the whistle. Chinese Police Officer No. 3226 and Chinese Detectives Chen Yonggui and Sun Shouzhong arrived and arrested Li and the other three, along with the destroyed teapot and mud statues, and took them to the Huishan Police Station. The police chief ordered them to be detained and sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District yesterday morning. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin presented the case, stating that the defendants were repeat offenders and requested an adjournment to investigate other cases. The evidence and court invoices were presented for inspection. The plaintiffs Fan Yimin, Xie Yongjin, and Tao Lianggen testified about their experiences. The defendants' testimonies were hesitant. Judge Wu Zehan ordered them to be returned to custody and reheard in seven days.

Inspection Report of Zhejiang Industrial Bank

The 41st inspection report of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank's issuance reserve showed that the Zhejiang Industrial Bank's issuance was completely separated from its business operations. The reserve was sufficient. On the 8th of this month, accountant Yan Ouke inspected and found that the gold reserve was over 60% and the guarantee reserve was below 40%. The numbers were as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued was 7,277,916.50 yuan. The total amount of the reserve was 7,277,916.50 yuan, including: the bank's own issuance was 4,127,916.50 yuan. The reserve was 2,839,916.50 yuan in cash and 1,288,000 yuan in guarantees. The amount used by peer bank was 3,150,000 yuan. The reserve was 2,388,000 yuan in cash and 763,000 yuan in guarantees.

Zhu Family Celebration Trial

Mr. Zhu Jingan of Xuanjing, Anhui, has been doing business in Shanghai for years and is well-known in the yarn industry. On the 9th of this month, he celebrated the 80th birthday of his father, Mr. Zhi Ren, and the wedding of his son, Dan Chu. Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Enemies Invade While Internal Strife Persists

— Yang An

▲Aggression Ambitions Just Beginning, But Strife Arises Within the Walls

More than half of the National Products Year has passed, how much progress has everyone reviewed? Just as you are ashamed and have nowhere to hide, the following is recorded in a Tokyo dispatch on October 31:

Recently, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has synthesized information from various sources, stating that the movement to boycott Japanese goods in China is gradually declining. Especially in North China, centered on Tianjin, Jinan, and Qingdao, the trend is completely unchanged from before the September 18th Incident. The Yangtze River area has also recently improved. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Bureau of Commerce, in view of Japan's lack of control over trade with China, must plan to establish a large company and grant it the exclusive privilege of trading with China. The investigation has already begun. All parties unanimously advocate that the establishment of a control mechanism for export companies to China is indeed necessary and will inevitably be realized soon.

This bad news of enemy invasion, sharpening its knives and pressing closer, is truly shocking to read, causing a cold sweat. However, at the same time, three pieces of news were received:

1. The dispute between the San Shan Guild Hall and the National Products Introduction Center, one side saying that it hindered the transport of national products, and the other side saying that it robbed people of their livelihood.

2. The conflict between the business community of Bengbu and the National Products Exhibition.

3. The business community of Xuzhou opposes the National Products Exhibition's dumping of national products.

These three pieces of news of internal strife were published in the newspaper at the same time, which cannot help but cause heartache and tears. The National Products Introduction Center said: "Those who hinder national products do not hinder the enemy, but hinder their own countrymen. Those who oppose national products do not oppose the enemy, but oppose their own countrymen. There is nothing more painful in the world than this." It is clearly for national products, for pure national products, that we are working hard to promote them, how can we bear to hinder them, to oppose them. In the midst of this advocacy of national products, there is such a phenomenon, if it is not due to misunderstanding, or ulterior motives, there is absolutely no such reason in the world. Even if there is a conflict of interest, one should suppress one's personal interests and take the overall situation into consideration, and even more so, one should not care about one's livelihood and exploit industry and commerce. In this era of national product crisis, when the situation is critical, all those with blood and conscience must broaden their horizons, shift their psychology of dealing with their own countrymen, and the concept of competition among their own industries, and focus on the outside world, defeat their own countrymen, and defeat their own industries. This is a despicable act, not a hero. If you are a hero, think about how to resist enemy goods? How can you prevent enemy goods from changing their appearance? How can you sanction unscrupulous merchants who sell Japanese goods in bulk? Put this kind of thinking, this kind of writing, this kind of strength, and use it all to resist enemy goods, then you can be worthy of society, worthy of the country, worthy of yourself.

National Products Talk

Are Goods Changing?

— He Gongxing

The biggest problem with national products is the change in appearance. The samples at the time of sale and the wholesale goods at the time of delivery have changed. The first product of a factory and the second or third product have changed even more. If it is said that one batch is better than another, this is a manifestation of the "improvement" and "progress" of goods, and national products have long been developed, so there is no need for the general public to advocate them. However, one batch is not as good as the previous batch. If sales are booming and goods are rushed, they are made worse and worse, until they are "concrete and micro." Then (returns) (fines) and disputes continue. What is the reason for this?

If it is said that manufacturers are all accustomed to cutting corners, it is inevitable to write them off in one stroke, which is a great injustice. Except for a few factory owners who disregard the overall situation and are eager to make profits, or inevitably make shoddy goods, almost all others hope that their products are excellent, so that people will be happy to buy and use them permanently, but the results often do not meet their wishes, and they still change a lot. This causes users to scold and manufacturers to lose heart. What is the reason for this? In short, the lack of standardization of raw materials is the reason.

In recent years, although my country's national products manufacturing industry has seen daily development, most of the various raw materials it needs still rely on foreign countries, and due to capital relations, it is often unable to purchase in large quantities. Most of them wait until they are needed to purchase them in small quantities. Since the raw materials are not neat, and the goods are often of poor quality, today German goods are used, and tomorrow French goods are used. Other British, Russian, Japanese and American goods are almost purchased in rotation. Since the producing areas are different, the properties are naturally difficult to be the same. To manufacture the same goods with different raw materials, is something that is not allowed in fact. This is the biggest reason for the change in the appearance of national products. People praise the Red Tin Pack cigarettes manufactured by the British American Tobacco Company, saying that they have not changed in decades, but it should be known that the raw materials used for making cigarettes have also been the same for decades.

Today, there are thousands of national products factories in Shanghai, and only a handful of manufacturers of raw materials. One is "finished products". If they are not sold well in place A, they can be sold to place B. If Zhang San does not buy them, they can be sold to Li Si. Regardless of whether the results are profitable or loss-making, there is no doubt that they will be sold. The other is "unfinished products". Not only cannot they be widely promoted, but they cannot be used alone. Buyers only need a few factories that need the goods. Because the raw materials used in the manufacture of raw materials also lack standardization, they have long caused buyers to doubt their suitability, and there are also foreign goods cheaper than ours, surrounding and competing for sale. If they cannot be sold, they will be stored in the factory, almost like dirt, and there is no other use. People are not stupid, so why bother to do this business without certainty?

Therefore, today, if we want national products to develop, we must first seek the consistency of national product goods, and if we want national product goods to be consistent, we must first seek the great development of the manufacturing raw materials industry. When using raw materials, we must identify the brand, and when manufacturing raw materials, we must identify the producing area. If we identify a certain raw material, we must compare which producing area is the most suitable. If it is not the material from that area, and the output is cut off, we must not easily change it. From then on, national products are standardized because of the raw materials, and the products are consistent from beginning to end.

National Products Discussion

A Frank Word to National Products Manufacturers for the National Products Exhibition

— Zhou Chengxun

By definition, the true purpose of the National Products Exhibition is to introduce domestic products in great detail and completeness, and to use a systematic and explanatory display method to enable all people to have the opportunity to recognize national products and to promote the idea of using national products as much as possible. However, if we examine the reality, national product exhibitions have been widely held in various places for the past seven or eight years, and national product manufacturers have worked hard to participate, has the above-mentioned effect been achieved? We will not talk about this very abstract question for the time being, but what we have felt in fact is a lot of painful reactions, and we have to give some honest advice to the national product manufacturers with a sincere attitude.

What kind of painful reactions? That is, some national product manufacturers simply do not understand the true meaning of the National Products Exhibition, and believe that participating in the National Products Exhibition is tantamount to temporarily setting up a sales place, and is tantamount to having an opportunity to clear out bottom goods. Therefore, they do things carelessly and only see profit. Over the years, the number of factories seeking profit has increased day by day at various national product exhibitions, and national product manufacturers who truly have ideological work have gradually decreased. In order to clear out bottom goods, local sales stores sell cheaply everywhere, which disrupts the stable market situation and causes dissatisfaction.

Recently, the business community in Bengbu shouted the slogan "Down with dumping, welcome exhibitions," and refused to allow local national product manufacturers to hold a National Products Exhibition. This is a good example. The reason they refused is: the rural economy in the mainland is declining to an irreparable degree, and the purchasing power is so

Notice to Readers

This magazine has been published for 44 issues. With the humble intention of promoting national products, it has won the praise of comrades. In the future, it intends to seek improvement in terms of materials and style. The materials should focus on practicality and not on empty talk, the writing style should be lively and not complicated, and the intention should be new. The style should be lively, and future submissions should focus on practicality, liveliness, and interest, so that readers can be effective as a guide. The number of words is two to three hundred, at most five hundred. Long articles with empty theories, ordinary language, no highlights, or those that are overly promotional will not be published. Please pay attention. (Editor)

weak, if they come with the purpose of clearing out inventory, not only will they go against the true meaning of the National Products Exhibition, but the dumping will also inevitably fail. To promote national products, it is not about selling, but about a complete exhibition. These words that hit the nail on the head are truly a lesson worth considering deeply and urgently reforming for national product factories.

We admire the spirit of all group organizations that lead national product factories to travel around, but we do have great regrets about the national product manufacturers who misunderstand the National Products Exhibition. I believe that the National Products Exhibition in the future must change its goals and earnestly implement the following principles:

1. Absolutely no selling. 2. Strictly review the degree of products produced by participating factories. 3. Introduce to the public the origin, quality, and manufacturing process of national products by various methods. 4. Guide local sales stores as much as possible on the advantages and disadvantages of sales and purchasing methods. 5. Establish national product showrooms everywhere to leave a lasting impression on the public.

By implementing the above five principles, the manufacturing, sales, and consumption aspects will all benefit greatly, and the true meaning of the National Products Exhibition will be clearly expressed. Otherwise, if we continue to hold exhibitions everywhere with the idea of clearing out inventory, resulting in rejection in the east and unwelcome in the west, how can we ask about the future of national products?

Contributing Opinions

Several National Product Substitutes That Need to Be Self-Made Urgently

— Pillow Wood

In recent years, efforts to manufacture national product substitutes have achieved good results, but there are still many substitutes that have not been self-made by Chinese factories and still only seek foreign goods. Now, I will list a few small industries that are in the greatest demand for urgent use, so that those who are ambitious and capable can quickly initiate preparations, research and manufacture, and save the outflow of profits.

▲Pen Holders and Nibs丨These are small items. Pen holders cost one dime per piece, and good ones cost three or four dimes. Nibs cost one cent per piece, and good ones cost four or five cents. Considering the number of people who use pens nationwide, including parties, governments, industries, businesses, schools, and institutions, there are a total of 15 million people who need them. It is estimated that each person consumes two pen holders and six nibs per year, then the annual consumption is as high as five or six million yuan. Perhaps the facts are even more than this. Now, these are all flowing into the hands of foreigners, how can we not recover them!

▲Galvanized Steel丨From the Shen Bao Yearbook, we can see that the import of galvanized steel reaches 800,000 dan per year, which is truly amazing. Among them, tinplate (i.e., lead skin) accounts for 409,000 dan, and galvanized wire accounts for 238,000 dan. And what about our country? Of course, there is no production at all. However, on the other hand, we see that the export of iron ore is 98,270,500 dan. Although it cannot be said that all of it has been turned into galvanized steel, if Chinese people can keep a part of it to make it themselves, it is also a lot of resistance.

▲Color Dyes丨Before the European War, indigo dyes were all supplied by Germany. After the war, Britain and Japan competed with each other. In the end, we have not yet produced our own goods, and we eat in foreign dyes worth 40 million taels of customs silver from the customs every year.

▲White Sugar丨Our country's local sugar is not pure white, so most of the high-quality white sugar is foreign goods. Although the current Republic of China Sugar Factory is set up by Chinese people, the results of competition are still unpredictable. I hope that those who are capable will help them.

▲Clocks丨Everyone, look at the clocks in your homes, most of them have the English words "Made in Japan". How terrible is this? Now I hope that China has clock-making factories, because this is not as precise as the watch industry. It does not matter if it is a little rougher. I hope that enthusiastic people will start doing it immediately.

▲Pencils丨Recently, it seems that a national product, Dahua Pencil, has been launched on the market. I am very fortunate, but it is impossible to resist Venus and Staedtler by relying on one company. Moreover, the factory is in Hong Kong, so the raw materials such as wood, stone houses, and sand may not be purely national products. It is not that the reporter is demanding, but I hope that someone will set up a factory in the inland of China near the forest. The graphite stored in our country is also very rich.

The above are just a few items that the reporter thinks are widely used and urgently needed. There are many others, but due to space limitations, I cannot list them all.

We Need Farmers to Recognize National Products

— Yao Xingshu

The fact that has already told us that the old China is a country with backward production. Therefore, today's compatriots are saying that they are advocating national products. However, unfortunately, the frequent foreign insults and internal chaos have formed a symbol of the bankruptcy of the rural economy in our country. No matter how loud you shout "advocating national products", the fact is that your national products are piled up in the warehouse and cannot be sold as much as possible. Of course, this economic control is more terrible than any other force. Therefore, if we want to promote national products, we should start by publicizing them in the rural areas.

We should not rely on waving flags and shouting in big cities to advocate national products. We should expand to rural areas to promote national products. We should not rely on a few advertisements to brag, and at the same time, we must consider the improvement of national products. Because in modern luxury cities, those decadent compatriots are mostly pretentious and deaf, and they are all full of standard foreigners. Their diet and daily life are all imported goods. Although there are also enlightened people who throw away their 1933-style foreign clothes and wear cheap and beautiful local cloth, readers! Please close your eyes and think about it. How many compatriots are really advocating national products?

Therefore, although this National Products Year has passed three-quarters of the time, we will not guess whether the past achievements have been successful. In the future, we may change a goal and move to the countryside to carry out activities. Although it is said that this year, our rural economy is bankrupt, and farmers can no longer afford to buy things, but I think at least we can make farmers have a considerable understanding of the two words "national products"!

Visit Notes

A Visit to a National Goods Wax Paper Factory

— Píng Nán

Visiting a national goods factory is one of the most joyful things for us. There are thoughts before the visit, and even more thoughts after the visit. Taking advantage of the Double Tenth Festival during this period of national crisis, I accepted an invitation from a friend to visit Mr. Chén Bǎo Shēng, the manager of Qín Yè Stationery Company in the South City, and asked him to take me on a tour of their national goods wax paper factory. He personally led me to Dǒngjiādù, crossed the river to the shore of Zhāngjiābāng, and then took a rickshaw east for about a mile to reach Hújiā Wooden Bridge. There, I saw a factory building in the field with the words "Qín Yè Stationery Company First Factory" written in large characters on the roof. The factory director, Mr. Lǐ Jìyún, greeted us warmly. Mr. Chén said that there was a second factory located at the foot of Tóngjūn Mountain in Tónglú County, Zhèjiāng, which collected raw materials and specialized in making the base paper for wax paper. It employed 150-160 male and female workers, all of whom were provided with food and lodging because the factory was located far from the village. This first factory was responsible for waxing and packaging. It employed only fifty-odd male and female workers. After speaking, he led me to the factory to tour the different sections. In the wax paper section, there were two four-open printing presses that printed the lines and the Three Children Flying a Kite trademark on the wax paper. This trademark was also known as the "Kite" brand. After the ink was dry, it was transported to the waxing room. The waxing room had four rooms, one for mixing and melting the wax materials, which only contained equipment such as boilers and iron boxes. The other three rooms contained six waxing machines, with stoves underneath the machines, burning quite hot. Two workers sat on the left and right sides of each machine. One worker took the printed paper with lines and fed it into the machine. As the machine turned, the other worker took the waxed paper out and lightly blew on it with their breath before placing it on a rack. This completed the waxing process. Mr. Chén said that the heat in the furnace had a specific limit; too much or too little would not work. Therefore, each machine was equipped with a thermometer to serve as a standard to avoid the unevenness of the wax on the paper. In addition, there were rooms for sorting and packing into tubes. Next, we went to the base paper section, where the papermaking tools were neatly arranged. Mr. Chén said that the base paper work only lasted five months each year, and all work stopped during hot weather because the base paper relied on gelatin, so it was impossible to work at that time. Next, we went to the colored chalk section, where we saw equipment such as gypsum melting stoves, grinding machines, and copper mold screening cabinets. After that, we went to the woodworking and steel tools section, where we saw the production and assembly of steel pens, steel plates, rubber sticks, silk screens, etc., which was quite busy. Mr. Chén then unfolded the lid of a fully assembled mimeograph machine, attached a printing frame covered with silk to protect the wax paper and allow for printing of an additional 100-200 sheets. The machine knob was equipped with a spring, so it would pop open automatically after printing. Half of the box also had a cover, which unfolded into an ink pad and was placed beside the box, making it very convenient to use the ink. Inside the box were compartments for storing rubber sticks, wax paper steel plates, steel pens, and other stationery. The outside of the box had leather buttons for easy carrying. Mr. Chén said that the steel plate had been improved many times and could now be used to write landscapes and figures. He showed several works, which were quite admirable. This is indeed a testament to the progress of national goods factories.

Random Thoughts on National Goods

— Qià

(I) Prelude

If we pay attention to daily life, there are often interesting materials in every detail. Here are some fragmentary impressions, collected because they are about national goods. Some are short but meaningful, and can also serve as a warning to us!

(II) Purely National Goods

Ms. Gé Chénghuì: Perhaps the only purely national goods in this place are these little babies!

(III) The Gate of the Grand Theater

The Grand Theater, known as the number one movie theater in the Far East, has all its internal equipment imported, but the two most prominent doors are made of Fújiàn lacquerware.

(IV) Summer

In the summer, I wore a long gown made of Indian silk. My friend ridiculed me as an "Ah Si" (a derogatory term for a servant). The listener took it to heart, and I was sweating profusely.

(V) Don't Advocate

Zhái Kègōng said: Standing from the perspective of the production industry, we should not advocate national goods, because we want to produce standard goods without relying on advocacy.

(VI) The Emotional Factor

Chéng Shǒuzhōng said: Relying solely on advocacy, the sales of national goods only have an emotional factor, which is temporary.

Extra Entertainment

One-Act Play

— Bā Líng

Time: Twelve o'clock on a certain day in 1933.

Location: The living room of a middle-class family.

Characters: Father, Mother, Son.

Mother: The weather is gradually getting colder. Huá'er's clothes are not yet ready. What kind of material do you think is most suitable to buy?

Father: Really, I forgot. Well, let's go buy it right after we eat. Fortunately, today is Thursday, and I took leave to stay at home. I think foreign goods are more authentic, and the price is only a little more expensive.

Huá'er: No, I heard the teacher say that this year is the National Goods Year. All Chinese people should buy Chinese goods and should not buy foreign goods. Moreover, current Chinese goods are much more advanced than before, and the price is also cheaper than foreign goods. If I wear foreign goods to school, I will be laughed at by my classmates...

Father: Oh! Let's buy Chinese goods!

Mother: Oh! This child is really ambitious. Let's go buy Chinese goods...

Special Education News

Reading the Outline of the National Basic Education Plan in Guǎngxī Province (II)

— Qín Fèngxiáng

(III) Methods: In countries with highly developed industry and commerce, young people are obsessed with vanity, abandoning the countryside and flocking to the cities. This causes the cities to become congested, while the countryside suffers from atrophy. Recently, the cities have also begun to decline. Therefore, those who are concerned about the times advocate a "return to the countryside" in the hope of reversing the situation. Now, industry and commerce in our country are depressed, and agriculture is declining. The reason for this is the exploitation by foreign powers, which affects the entire country. This is completely different from other countries where there is partial, abnormal development, causing the countries to poison themselves. Our countryside has abundant surplus labor, and the construction of industry and commerce is just beginning. Therefore, the plan for now is to enable all surplus labor to have the opportunity to engage in production, and not to be wasted. This alone would be a great blessing. There is no need to study whether the children of farmers should always be farmers, or the children of industrialists should always be industrialists. It doesn't matter if agriculture transforms into industry, industry into commerce, or commerce into agriculture. The original proposal hopes that young students will cooperate with labor and guide the people to assist the government in construction, which is a good idea. However, party hacks, corrupt officials, education pests, gangsters, and bandits cannot be considered professions, and ambitious young people would not deign to be them. The original proposal lists the countryside, shops, and factories, which already encompass all occupations. However, they are all unified under the phrase "return to," as if all ambitious young people in society are leaving their current occupations to pursue something else. They do not know that it is because they are forced by external forces and cannot easily find employment. Also, what needs construction now is not only the countryside. Young people are even more important than children in assisting the government. Therefore, I propose the following wording: "1. Guide children, young people, and adults in developing diligent habits, so that they can devote themselves to productive enterprises and assist the government in establishing the foundation for social and economic construction. 2. Guide children, young people, and adults in developing disciplined actions, so that they can devote themselves to autonomous undertakings and assist the government in establishing the foundation for social and political construction. 3. Guide children, young people, and adults in developing creative interests, so that they can devote themselves to the national rejuvenation and assist the government in establishing the foundation for social and cultural construction."

(IV) Work: At the beginning of the implementation of universal education in various countries, the schooling period was very short. Those who blindly admire the current state of advanced countries and advocate extending the length of compulsory education in our country are indulging in excessive expectations. Now, the original proposal takes into account the reality and advocates shortening the length of schooling, which is a very good idea. However, since the name "national basic education" has already been proposed to encompass the entire system, there is no need to retain the old names of "compulsory education" and the illogical "mass education." This would avoid giving narrow-minded people the opportunity to arbitrarily establish factions and divide authority. Children aged six to nine have relatively poor learning abilities. Providing them with the education of the first and second grades of primary school yields limited results and is easily forgotten. When they grow older, it will be of no practical use, and some of these children are very suitable for further education. The connection of future courses will definitely be difficult. Also, militia, self-government, and cooperation are to adults what language, arithmetic, and nature are to children. These should be specified separately in the curriculum or training matters. There is no need to elaborate on them in this article. Therefore, I propose the following wording: "1. Children aged six to ten should be free to attend school and receive national basic education in ordinary primary schools. 2. Children aged ten to sixteen should be forced to attend school and receive two years of national basic education. 3. Young people aged sixteen to twenty should be forced to attend school and receive one year of national basic education. 4. Adults over the age of twenty should receive national basic education for a corresponding period." (To be continued)

Out of Town

The Ministry of Education Explains the Phased Implementation of the School System

The following are three orders from the Ministry of Education regarding the explanation of the school system, curriculum, and methods for retroactive qualification: (1) The Beijing Municipal Social Bureau submitted a proposal that the principals of private schools should not be selected as directors of the school to clarify powers and avoid disputes. The Ministry of Education explained that the principals of private schools are elected by the board of directors, and the directors can also be elected as principals. If disputes arise in the board of directors, they should be handled in accordance with Article 12, Section 2 of the Regulations for Private Schools. (2) The Shānxī Education Department, according to the Provincial Fourth Normal School, requested whether the curriculum for new normal school students should still be handled in accordance with the Provisional Standards for Secondary School Curriculum, Senior High School Normal Department. The Ministry of Education instructed that before the official standards for the normal school curriculum are promulgated, they should still follow the Provisional Standards for Senior High School Normal Department Curriculum. (3) Xuē Yī'è requested the approval of retroactive recognition of the graduation qualifications of Private Fùdàn University. The Ministry of Education instructed that the applicant graduated before the school was formally recognized by the former Beijing Ministry of Education. Their graduation qualifications should not be retroactively recognized according to the old practice of the former ministry. However, they may follow the relief measures in Item 6 of the standards for retroactive qualification established in this year's Instruction No. 8699 of this Ministry and must undergo a qualification examination. You are hereby informed.

The Opening of the Zhèjiāng Provincial Secondary School Principals' Conference ▲Yesterday at 9:00 AM

(Háng Conf.) The Provincial Secondary School Principals' Conference convened by the Zhèjiāng Provincial Department of Education is scheduled to hold its opening ceremony at 9:00 AM today. In addition to the principals of the provincial secondary schools, as well as Director Chén, the secretary, section chiefs, editors, and assigned staff of the Education Department, representatives of the Provincial Party Headquarters were invited to attend and provide guidance. Governor Lǔ of the Provincial Government and Inspector Dài Yì of the Ministry of Education are expected to attend and deliver speeches. The opening ceremony is as follows: (1) All stand at attention. (2) Sing the Party song. (3) Pay the highest respect to the national flag, Party flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen. (4) The chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will. (5) Silence. (6) The chairman delivers the opening speech. (7) The representative of the Provincial Party Headquarters gives a speech. (8) The governor of the Provincial Government gives a speech. (9) The inspector of the Ministry of Education gives a speech. The general meeting will be held at 1:00 PM, and the group meetings will be held after 2:00 PM. It is reported that the proposals submitted to the department for review and compilation can be divided into four categories: A. Teaching category (11 items), B. Moral education category (1 item), C. Administrative category (17 items), D. Financial category (16 items).

(Hángzhōu Correspondence) The Zhè Education Department convened a conference of provincial secondary school principals at 9:00 AM on the 8th in the auditorium of the department. Those who attended were: Provincial Party Headquarters representative Luo Xiaotian, Ministry of Education Inspector Dai, Director of Education Department Chén Bùléi, and Secretary Section Chiefs Qian Jiazhi and Luo Dixian, etc., as well as more than 20 principals of various secondary schools, including Ye Suchong, Lin Ben, and Zhang Yinian. The Education Department also assigned staff members such as Hu Changfeng to attend. Chén Bùléi presided over the meeting. After the ceremony, he delivered the opening speech, followed by speeches from Luo Xiaotian, the representative of the Provincial Party Headquarters, Lǔ Dípíng, the governor of the Provincial Government, and Dai Xia, the inspector of the Ministry of Education. Finally, speeches were given by Ye Suchong, the principal of Hángzhōu High School, Fang Hao, the principal of Jīnhuá Middle School, and Yu Kuàng, the principal of the Experimental Agricultural School.

The first general meeting was held at 1:00 PM, with 31 attendees. Director Chén presided over the meeting and discussed the following matters: (1) A decision was made to hold group meetings, divided into four groups: administration, teaching, moral education, and finance. The administration group and the finance group were combined into one category, and the teaching group and the moral education group were combined into another category. The two categories would not meet at the same time to avoid conflicts. (2) All 52 proposals were assigned to the respective groups for review, including 11 items for the teaching group, 1 item for the moral education group, 22 items for the administration group, and 18 items for the finance group. (3) Each principal, except for the personnel attending from the Education Department, freely chose two groups (list omitted). (4) Qian Junfu was designated to convene the teaching group, Lin Lishu to convene the moral education group, Lu Buqing to convene the administration group, and Li Zihan to convene the finance group. The administration group and the finance group held group meetings after 2:00 PM. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. In the evening at 7:00 PM, the Education Department's secretary hosted a public banquet for the principals at the YMCA. (Sent on the 8th)

The Educational Film Association Plans to Compile the China Film Yearbook

After the China Educational Film Association previously passed the resolution to compile the China Film Yearbook, it organized an editorial committee to be responsible for compiling the yearbook. It has already sent a letter to hire Chén Lìfū as the chief editor, and Wáng Pínglíng and Dài Cè as full-time editors. Lì Jiāxiáng, Lǐ Jǐngbì, Pān Gōngzhǎn, and Zhāng Chángrén are serving as editors, separately collecting materials and starting to edit. Regarding the solicitation of foreign materials, the China Educational Film Association plans to send letters to the embassies and consulates stationed abroad, and the Ministries of Interior and Education of various countries, requesting them to send regulations and rules regarding films for reference. It is also reported that the full-time editor Dài Cè has now gone to Shànghǎi to conduct on-site investigations of various film companies in Shànghǎi and collect books that can be used as reference materials for compiling the film yearbook. It is planned to print 5,000 copies of this yearbook, with the final draft due by the end of February and publication by the end of March.
